The proposed framework differs by utilizing small LLMs (3B-7B parameters) that are open-source and designed for comprehensive teacher support, including the generation of customized teaching materials and AI-assisted assessments. The contribution lies in the introduction of a novel end-to-end system that integrates Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) and Context-Augmented Generation (CAG), featuring an interactive refinement loop for educator involvement and an auxiliary verifier LLM for content reliability. The methodology was validated through a deployment in a college physics course, demonstrating that the framework can effectively generate pedagogically appropriate content while maintaining affordability and privacy, achieving performance comparable to larger models for specific instructional tasks.

SGuard-v1: Safety Guardrail for Large Language Models
Authors: JoonHo Lee, HyeonMin Cho, Jaewoong Yun, Hyunjae Lee, JunKyu Lee, Juree Seok
First: 2025-11-16T08:15:54+00:00 · Latest: 2025-11-16T08:15:54+00:00
Comments: Technical Report
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present SGuard-v1, a lightweight safety guardrail for Large Language Models (LLMs), which comprises two specialized models to detect harmful content and screen adversarial prompts in human-AI conversational settings. The first component, ContentFilter, is trained to identify safety risks in LLM prompts and responses in accordance with the MLCommons hazard taxonomy, a comprehensive framework for trust and safety assessment of AI. The second component, JailbreakFilter, is trained with a carefully designed curriculum over integrated datasets and findings from prior work on adversarial prompting, covering 60 major attack types while mitigating false-unsafe classification. SGuard-v1 is built on the 2B-parameter Granite-3.3-2B-Instruct model that supports 12 languages. We curate approximately 1.4 million training instances from both collected and synthesized data and perform instruction tuning on the base model, distributing the curated data across the two component according to their designated functions. Through extensive evaluation on public and proprietary safety benchmarks, SGuard-v1 achieves state-of-the-art safety performance while remaining lightweight, thereby reducing deployment overhead. SGuard-v1 also improves interpretability for downstream use by providing multi-class safety predictions and their binary confidence scores. We release the SGuard-v1 under the Apache-2.0 License to enable further research and practical deployment in AI safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SGuard-v1：大型语言模型的安全护栏
我们提出了SGuard-v1，一种轻量级的安全护栏，旨在为大型语言模型（LLMs）提供保护，包含两个专门模型用于检测有害内容和筛选人机对话中的对抗性提示。第一个组件ContentFilter经过训练，能够根据MLCommons危害分类法识别LLM提示和响应中的安全风险，这是一个全面的AI信任与安全评估框架。第二个组件JailbreakFilter则通过精心设计的课程，结合集成数据集和先前对抗性提示研究的发现进行训练，涵盖60种主要攻击类型，同时减轻误判为不安全的情况。SGuard-v1基于支持12种语言的2B参数Granite-3.3-2B-Instruct模型构建。我们从收集和合成的数据中整理了大约140万个训练实例，并对基础模型进行了指令调优，根据各自的功能将整理的数据分配到两个组件中。通过对公共和专有安全基准的广泛评估，SGuard-v1在保持轻量的同时实现了最先进的安全性能，从而减少了部署开销。SGuard-v1还通过提供多类安全预测及其二元置信度分数，提高了下游使用的可解释性。我们在Apache-2.0许可证下发布SGuard-v1，以促进AI安全领域的进一步研究和实际部署。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing concern of safety in human-AI interactions, particularly with Large Language Models (LLMs), which can produce harmful content. Previous methods lacked comprehensive frameworks for assessing safety risks and often resulted in high false-positive rates in identifying adversarial prompts. The proposed SGuard-v1 introduces a dual-component system, consisting of ContentFilter and JailbreakFilter, which effectively identifies safety risks and screens adversarial prompts while minimizing false classifications. This approach is well-motivated by the need for reliable safety measures in AI applications. The methodology involves training on a large dataset of approximately 1.4 million instances, utilizing instruction tuning on a robust 2B-parameter model. SGuard-v1 demonstrates state-of-the-art safety performance on various benchmarks, supporting its goal of enhancing safety in AI deployments while maintaining a lightweight structure for easier implementation.
本研究针对大型语言模型（LLMs）中对有害内容和对抗性提示的安全措施需求日益增长的问题。以往的方法缺乏全面的安全风险评估框架，且常常导致较高的误报率。提出的SGuard-v1引入了一个双组件系统，包括ContentFilter和JailbreakFilter，能够有效识别安全风险并减轻对抗性攻击，同时保持轻量化结构。该方法具有良好的动机，因为它利用了大约140万实例的强大训练数据集，并整合了先前研究的发现以增强性能。该方法在各种基准测试中展示了最先进的安全性能，支持其提高人工智能安全性和确保高效部署的目标。
GRAPHTEXTACK: A Realistic Black-Box Node Injection Attack on LLM-Enhanced GNNs
Authors: Jiaji Ma, Puja Trivedi, Danai Koutra
Venue: AAAI 2026
First: 2025-11-16T02:42:48+00:00 · Latest: 2025-11-16T02:42:48+00:00
Comments: AAAI 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Text-attributed graphs (TAGs), which combine structural and textual node information, are ubiquitous across many domains. Recent work integrates Large Language Models (LLMs) with Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) to jointly model semantics and structure, resulting in more general and expressive models that achieve state-of-the-art performance on TAG benchmarks. However, this integration introduces dual vulnerabilities: GNNs are sensitive to structural perturbations, while LLM-derived features are vulnerable to prompt injection and adversarial phrasing. While existing adversarial attacks largely perturb structure or text independently, we find that uni-modal attacks cause only modest degradation in LLM-enhanced GNNs. Moreover, many existing attacks assume unrealistic capabilities, such as white-box access or direct modification of graph data. To address these gaps, we propose GRAPHTEXTACK, the first black-box, multi-modal{, poisoning} node injection attack for LLM-enhanced GNNs. GRAPHTEXTACK injects nodes with carefully crafted structure and semantics to degrade model performance, operating under a realistic threat model without relying on model internals or surrogate models. To navigate the combinatorial, non-differentiable search space of connectivity and feature assignments, GRAPHTEXTACK introduces a novel evolutionary optimization framework with a multi-objective fitness function that balances local prediction disruption and global graph influence. Extensive experiments on five datasets and two state-of-the-art LLM-enhanced GNN models show that GRAPHTEXTACK significantly outperforms 12 strong baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GRAPHTEXTACK：一种针对LLM增强GNN的现实黑箱节点注入攻击
文本属性图（TAG）结合了结构和文本节点信息，广泛应用于多个领域。最近的研究将大型语言模型（LLM）与图神经网络（GNN）结合，以共同建模语义和结构，从而实现更通用和更具表现力的模型，在TAG基准测试中取得了最先进的性能。然而，这种集成引入了双重脆弱性：GNN对结构扰动敏感，而LLM派生特征易受提示注入和对抗性措辞的影响。虽然现有的对抗攻击主要独立扰动结构或文本，但我们发现单模态攻击对LLM增强的GNN造成的降级仅为适度。此外，许多现有攻击假设不切实际的能力，例如白箱访问或直接修改图数据。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了GRAPHTEXTACK，这是首个针对LLM增强GNN的黑箱多模态节点注入攻击。GRAPHTEXTACK通过精心设计的结构和语义注入节点，以降低模型性能，操作在一个现实的威胁模型下，而不依赖于模型内部或替代模型。为了导航连接性和特征分配的组合非可微搜索空间，GRAPHTEXTACK引入了一种新颖的进化优化框架，具有多目标适应度函数，平衡局部预测干扰和全局图影响。在五个数据集和两个最先进的LLM增强GNN模型上的广泛实验表明，GRAPHTEXTACK显著优于12个强基线。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the vulnerabilities of Large Language Model (LLM)-enhanced Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) when applied to text-attributed graphs (TAGs), which combine structural and textual information. Previous methods primarily focused on uni-modal attacks that either altered structure or text independently, leading to limited effectiveness against LLM-enhanced GNNs and often assuming unrealistic attack capabilities. The proposed GRAPHTEXTACK approach differs by introducing a black-box, multi-modal node injection attack that operates under a realistic threat model, effectively degrading model performance without needing internal model access. This paper contributes a novel evolutionary optimization framework with a multi-objective fitness function to navigate the complex search space of node connectivity and feature assignments. Experimental results demonstrate that GRAPHTEXTACK significantly outperforms 12 strong baselines across five datasets and two state-of-the-art LLM-enhanced GNN models, validating its effectiveness in real-world scenarios.
本研究探讨了在文本属性图（TAGs）中应用增强型大语言模型（LLM）的图神经网络（GNNs）时的脆弱性。以往的方法主要集中在单模态攻击上，分别改变结构或文本，导致对增强型LLM-GNN的效果有限，并且通常假设不切实际的条件，如白盒访问。所提出的方法GRAPHTEXTACK是一种黑盒多模态节点注入攻击，旨在通过结构和语义的结合修改来降低模型性能，且在现实威胁模型下运行。该方法采用创新的进化优化框架，结合多目标适应度函数，有效地导航连接性和特征分配的复杂搜索空间。对五个数据集和两个最先进的LLM增强GNN模型的实验结果表明，GRAPHTEXTACK显著优于12种强基线方法，证实了其在解决识别的脆弱性方面的有效性。
